and the histogram output is written to topic \"streams-wordcount-processor-output\" where each record\n * is an updated count of a single word.\n * <p>\n * Before running this example you must create the input topic and the output topic (e.g. via\n * {@code bin/kafka-topics.sh --create ...}), and write some data to the input topic (e.g. via\n * {@code bin/kafka-console-producer.sh}). Otherwise you won't see any data arriving in the output topic.\n */\npublic final class WordCountProcessorDemo {\n    static class WordCountProcessor implements Processor<String, String, String, String> {\n        private KeyValueStore<String, Integer> kvStore;\n\n        @Override\n        public void init(final ProcessorContext<String, String> context) {\n            context.schedule(Duration.ofSeconds(1), PunctuationType.STREAM_TIME, timestamp -> {\n                try (final KeyValueIterator<String, Integer> iter = kvStore.all()) {\n                    System.out.println(\"----------- \" + timestamp + \" ----------- \");\n\n                    while (iter.hasNext()) {\n                        final KeyValue<String, Integer> entry = iter.next();\n\n                        System.out.println(\"[\" + entry.key + \", \" + entry.value + \"]\");\n\n                        context.forward(new Record<>(entry.key, entry.value.toString(), timestamp));\n                    }\n                }\n            });\n            kvStore = context.getStateStore(\"Counts\");\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public void process(final Record<String, String> record) {\n            final String[] words = record.value().toLowerCase(Locale.getDefault()).split(\"\\\\W+\");\n\n            for (final String word : words) {\n                final Integer oldValue = kvStore.get(word);\n\n                if (oldValue == null) {\n                    kvStore.put(word, 1);\n                } else {\n                    kvStore.put(word, oldValue + 1);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public void close() {\n            // close any resources managed by this processor\n            // Note: Do not close any StateStores as these are managed by the library\n        }\n    }\n\n    public static void main(final String[] args) throws IOException {\n        final Properties props = new Properties();","numLines":100,"startLine":1,"totalLines":154}}}

Processor<KIn, Change<VIn>, KIn, Change<VOut>>\\n- Transforms values in KTable while managing state and changelog semantics\\n\\n### Processor API Base Classes\\n\\n**Processor** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/Processor.java): Core interface for processing records with key and value type parameters and transformation capabilities.\\n\\n**ProcessorSupplier** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/ProcessorSupplier.java): Factory interface that creates Processor instances, enabling stateless and stateful processor creation.\\n\\n**FixedKeyProcessor**: Specialized processor for operations that don't change keys, enabling optimization for key-preserving transformations.\\n\\n**FixedKeyProcessorSupplier**: Factory for FixedKeyProcessor instances.\\n\\n**ContextualProcessor**: Base class extending Processor with convenience methods for accessing ProcessorContext.\\n\\n**ContextualFixedKeyProcessor**: Base class extending FixedKeyProcessor with context convenience methods.\\n\\n**Record** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/Record.java): Encapsulates key-value records with timestamp and headers for processing.\\n\\n**FixedKeyRecord**: Specialized record type Replace DSL method calls (e.g., stream.map(mapper)) with direct Topology construction\\n2. Create custom ProcessorSupplier or FixedKeyProcessorSupplier implementations\\n3. Implement the Processor interface with custom process() logic\\n4. Access ProcessorContext for state store management and record forwarding\\n5. (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/Processor.java): Core interface for processing records with key and value type parameters and transformation capabilities.\\n\\n**ProcessorSupplier** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/ProcessorSupplier.java): Factory interface that creates Processor instances, enabling stateless and stateful processor creation.\\n\\n**FixedKeyProcessor**: Specialized processor for operations that don't change keys, enabling optimization for key-preserving transformations.\\n\\n**FixedKeyProcessorSupplier**: Factory for FixedKeyProcessor instances.\\n\\n**ContextualProcessor**: Base class extending Processor with convenience methods for accessing ProcessorContext.\\n\\n**ContextualFixedKeyProcessor**: Base class extending FixedKeyProcessor with context convenience methods.\\n\\n**Record** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/processor/api/Record.java): Encapsulates key-value records with timestamp and headers for processing.\\n\\n**FixedKeyRecord**: Specialized record type for fixed-key operations.\\n\\n### Example Implementations\\n\\n**WordCountDemo** (streams/examples/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/examples/wordcount/WordCountDemo.java): High-level DSL example using flatMapValues(), groupBy(), and count() operations. Demonstrates the declarative approach to stream processing.\\n\\n**WordCountProcessorDemo** (streams/examples/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/examples/wordcount/WordCountProcessorDemo.java): Low-level Processor API implementation of word count. Implements Processor<String, String, String, String> directly, managing a KeyValueStore for state management. Shows how to use context.schedule() for punctuation and custom state store operations.\\n\\n### Aggregation Operations\\n\\n**KStreamAggregate** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamAggregate.java): Implements KStreamAggProcessorSupplier for stream aggregations, managing state stores and enabling custom initialization and aggregation logic through Initializer and Aggregator interfaces.\\n\\n**KStreamAggProcessorSupplier** (streams/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/streams/kstream/internals/KStreamAggProcessorSupplier.java): Interface for aggregation processor suppliers with state store management.\\n\\n### Migration Path\\n\\nTo migrate from DSL to Processor API:\\n1. Replace DSL method calls (e.g., stream.map(mapper)) with direct Topology construction\\n2. Create custom ProcessorSupplier or FixedKeyProcessorSupplier implementations\\n3. Implement the Processor interface with custom process() logic\\n4. Access ProcessorContext for state store management and record forwarding\\n5. Use context.schedule() for punctuation and state store operations\\n6. Manage state stores manually via context.getStateStore() instead of relying on DSL-managed stores\\n7. Handle state changelog semantics manually in table operations\\n\\nThe mapping from DSL to Processor API is consistent across all operations, with ProcessorSupplier implementations creating Processor instances that execute the transformation logic via ContextualProcessor extensions.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
